 In Ceron village of the district, a farmer was brutally beaten up for two hours by a mob

 iske liye fefde ke cancer kii koshikaayen sabase pehle us protein ko khatm kar detii he, jo use padosi koshikaon se jode rakhti he
 Angeliki Maliri, lead researcher at the Cancer Research UK Manchester Institute at the University of Manchester, UK, said, 'this research revealed for the first time how lung cancer cells occupy the cell recycle process and differentiate it from neighboring cells
 
 'nishkarsh main khulaasa hua he ki koshikaon ko aapas main jode rakhane kaa kaam ek protein (TIMA1) karata he
 When there is a disturbance in the repair process of cells, TIMA1 is eliminated and the cell is isolated
 biimaar koshikaon kii jagah swasth koshikaayen leti rahati hai
 But in the case of lung cancer, this process goes unchecked, resulting in massive destruction of TIMA1 and thus the proliferation of cancer cells
 ricycle kii is prakriya ko niyantrit kar fefde ke cancer ko failane se roka ja saktaa he
 Nell Barry of Cancer Research UK said, "research of this type of early stage is very important to find a cure and one day it will come, when the spread of cancer cells will be completely controlled and a permanent solution to cancer will be found
"
